This allows us to see (roughly) what browsers are in use in the wild, along with other useful metrics such as OS and device. If you'd like to disable analytics, you can simply include the following global before including Video.js via the free CDN:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-text-html-basic notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"\u0026lt;script\u0026gt;window.HELP_IMPROVE_VIDEOJS = false;\u0026lt;/script\u0026gt;\"\u003e\u003cpre\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e\u0026lt;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003escript\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-smi\"\u003ewindow\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e.\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003eHELP_IMPROVE_VIDEOJS\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003e=\u003c/span\u003e \u003cspan class=\"pl-c1\"\u003efalse\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e;\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e\u0026lt;/\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-ent\"\u003escript\u003c/span\u003e\u003cspan class=\"pl-kos\"\u003e\u0026gt;\u003c/span\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\u003c/div\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eAlternatively, you can include Video.js by getting it from \u003ca href=\"https://videojs.com/getting-started/#install-via-npm\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003enpm\u003c/a\u003e, downloading from \u003ca href=\"https://github.com/videojs/video.js/releases\"\u003eGitHub releases\u003c/a\u003e or by including it via \u003ca href=\"https://unpkg.com\" rel=\"nofollow\"\u003eunpkg\u003c/a\u003e or another JavaScript CDN like CDNjs. <a href="https://greenkeeper.io/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/3149c1ec6befc3c036ba11e2ab35b629a545d76f9d8ede7c331bd50bf2630f6f/68747470733a2f2f6261646765732e677265656e6b65657065722e696f2f766964656f6a732f766964656f2e6a732e737667" alt="Greenkeeper badge" data-canonical-src="https://badges.greenkeeper.io/videojs/video.js.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
<a href="http://slack.videojs.com" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/b8004463fad3cc50ed27201812c5a030241f3d7b5f7506c79d7e0be046aad138/687474703a2f2f736c61636b2e766964656f6a732e636f6d2f62616467652e737667" alt="Slack Status" data-canonical-src="http://slack.videojs.com/badge.svg" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://nodei.co/npm/video.js/" rel="nofollow"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/c7a242cf1516446e038aec14d475845a28b77121e696148090dee4384e6da1ed/68747470733a2f2f6e6f6465692e636f2f6e706d2f766964656f2e6a732e706e673f646f776e6c6f6164733d7472756526646f776e6c6f616452616e6b3d74727565" alt="NPM" data-canonical-src="https://nodei.co/npm/video.js.png?downloads=true&amp;downloadRank=true" style="max-width: 100%;"></a></p>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Video.js is a web video player built from the ground up for an HTML5 world. It supports HTML5 video and Media Source Extensions, as well as other playback techs like YouTube and Vimeo (through <a href="https://videojs.com/plugins/" rel="nofollow">plugins</a>). It supports video playback on desktops and mobile devices. This project was started mid 2010, and the player is now used on over <del>50,000</del> <del>100,000</del> <del>200,000</del> <del>400,000</del> <a href="https://trends.builtwith.com/media/VideoJS" rel="nofollow">700,000 websites</a>.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-table-of-contents" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#table-of-contents"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Table of Contents</h2>
<ul dir="auto">

<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-quick-start" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#quick-start"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Quick Start</h2>
<p dir="auto">Thanks to the awesome folks over at <a href="https://www.fastly.com/" rel="nofollow">Fastly</a>, there's a free, CDN hosted version of Video.js that anyone can use. Add these tags to your document's <code>&lt;head&gt;</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;link href=&quot;//vjs.zencdn.net/8.3.0/video-js.min.css&quot; rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot;&gt;
&lt;script src=&quot;//vjs.zencdn.net/8.3.0/video.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">link</span> <span class="pl-c1">href</span>="<span class="pl-s">//vjs.zencdn.net/8.3.0/video-js.min.css</span>" <span class="pl-c1">rel</span>="<span class="pl-s">stylesheet</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">//vjs.zencdn.net/8.3.0/video.min.js</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p dir="auto">For the latest version of video.js and URLs to use, check out the <a href="https://videojs.com/getting-started/" rel="nofollow">Getting Started</a> page on our website.</p>
</blockquote>
<p dir="auto">Video.js version 7 (and newer) CDN builds do not send any data to Google Analytics.</p>
<p dir="auto">In older versions of Video.js (6 and earlier), in the <code>vjs.zencdn.net</code> CDN-hosted versions we include a <a href="https://github.com/videojs/cdn/blob/master/src/analytics.js">stripped down Google Analytics pixel</a> that tracks a random sampling (currently 1%) of players loaded from the CDN. This allows us to see (roughly) what browsers are in use in the wild, along with other useful metrics such as OS and device. If you'd like to disable analytics, you can simply include the following global before including Video.js via the free CDN:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;script&gt;window.HELP_IMPROVE_VIDEOJS = false;&lt;/script&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-smi">window</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">HELP_IMPROVE_VIDEOJS</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">false</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Alternatively, you can include Video.js by getting it from <a href="https://videojs.com/getting-started/#install-via-npm" rel="nofollow">npm</a>, downloading from <a href="https://github.com/videojs/video.js/releases">GitHub releases</a> or by including it via <a href="https://unpkg.com" rel="nofollow">unpkg</a> or another JavaScript CDN like CDNjs. These releases <em>do not</em> include Google Analytics tracking at all.</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;!-- unpkg : use the latest version of Video.js --&gt;
&lt;link href=&quot;https://unpkg.com/video.js/dist/video-js.min.css&quot; rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot;&gt;
&lt;script src=&quot;https://unpkg.com/video.js/dist/video.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;

&lt;!-- unpkg : use a specific version of Video.js (change the version numbers as necessary) --&gt;
&lt;link href=&quot;https://unpkg.com/video.js@8.3.0/dist/video-js.min.css&quot; rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot;&gt;
&lt;script src=&quot;https://unpkg.com/video.js@8.3.0/dist/video.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;

&lt;!-- cdnjs : use a specific version of Video.js (change the version numbers as necessary) --&gt;
&lt;link href=&quot;https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/video.js/8.3.0/video-js.min.css&quot; rel=&quot;stylesheet&quot;&gt;
&lt;script src=&quot;https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/video.js/8.3.0/video.min.js&quot;&gt;&lt;/script&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- unpkg : use the latest version of Video.js --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">link</span> <span class="pl-c1">href</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://unpkg.com/video.js/dist/video-js.min.css</span>" <span class="pl-c1">rel</span>="<span class="pl-s">stylesheet</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://unpkg.com/video.js/dist/video.min.js</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- unpkg : use a specific version of Video.js (change the version numbers as necessary) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">link</span> <span class="pl-c1">href</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://unpkg.com/video.js@8.3.0/dist/video-js.min.css</span>" <span class="pl-c1">rel</span>="<span class="pl-s">stylesheet</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://unpkg.com/video.js@8.3.0/dist/video.min.js</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>

<span class="pl-c">&lt;!-- cdnjs : use a specific version of Video.js (change the version numbers as necessary) --&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">link</span> <span class="pl-c1">href</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/video.js/8.3.0/video-js.min.css</span>" <span class="pl-c1">rel</span>="<span class="pl-s">stylesheet</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/video.js/8.3.0/video.min.js</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">script</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">Next, using Video.js is as simple as creating a <code>&lt;video&gt;</code> element, but with an additional <code>data-setup</code> attribute. At a minimum, this attribute must have a value of <code>'{}'</code>, but it can include any Video.js <a href="https://videojs.com/guides/options/" rel="nofollow">options</a> - just make sure it contains valid JSON!</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-text-html-basic notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="&lt;video
    id=&quot;my-player&quot;
    class=&quot;video-js&quot;
    controls
    preload=&quot;auto&quot;
    poster=&quot;//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.png&quot;
    data-setup='{}'&gt;
  &lt;source src=&quot;//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.mp4&quot; type=&quot;video/mp4&quot;&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
  &lt;source src=&quot;//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.webm&quot; type=&quot;video/webm&quot;&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
  &lt;source src=&quot;//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.ogv&quot; type=&quot;video/ogg&quot;&gt;&lt;/source&gt;
  &lt;p class=&quot;vjs-no-js&quot;&gt;
    To view this video please enable JavaScript, and consider upgrading to a
    web browser that
    &lt;a href=&quot;https://videojs.com/html5-video-support/&quot; target=&quot;_blank&quot;&gt;
      supports HTML5 video
    &lt;/a&gt;
  &lt;/p&gt;
&lt;/video&gt;"><pre><span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">video</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">id</span>="<span class="pl-s">my-player</span>"
    <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">video-js</span>"
    <span class="pl-c1">controls</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">preload</span>="<span class="pl-s">auto</span>"
    <span class="pl-c1">poster</span>="<span class="pl-s">//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.png</span>"
    <span class="pl-c1">data-setup</span>='<span class="pl-s">{}</span>'<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">source</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.mp4</span>" <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">video/mp4</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">source</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">source</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.webm</span>" <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">video/webm</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">source</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">source</span> <span class="pl-c1">src</span>="<span class="pl-s">//vjs.zencdn.net/v/oceans.ogv</span>" <span class="pl-c1">type</span>="<span class="pl-s">video/ogg</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span><span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">source</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span> <span class="pl-c1">class</span>="<span class="pl-s">vjs-no-js</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
    To view this video please enable JavaScript, and consider upgrading to a
    web browser that
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;</span><span class="pl-ent">a</span> <span class="pl-c1">href</span>="<span class="pl-s">https://videojs.com/html5-video-support/</span>" <span class="pl-c1">target</span>="<span class="pl-s">_blank</span>"<span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
      supports HTML5 video
    <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">a</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">p</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">&lt;/</span><span class="pl-ent">video</span><span class="pl-kos">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">When the page loads, Video.js will find this element and automatically setup a player in its place.</p>
<p dir="auto">If you don't want to use automatic setup, you can leave off the <code>data-setup</code> attribute and initialize a <code>&lt;video&gt;</code> element manually using the <code>videojs</code> function:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var player = videojs('my-player');"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">player</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">videojs</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-player'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>videojs</code> function also accepts an <code>options</code> object and a callback to be invoked
when the player is ready:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="var options = {};

var player = videojs('my-player', options, function onPlayerReady() {
  videojs.log('Your player is ready!');

  // In this context, `this` is the player that was created by Video.js.
  this.play();

  // How about an event listener?
  this.on('ended', function() {
    videojs.log('Awww...over so soon?!');
  });
});"><pre><span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span><span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<span class="pl-k">var</span> <span class="pl-s1">player</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">videojs</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'my-player'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-s1">options</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">onPlayerReady</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
  <span class="pl-s1">videojs</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Your player is ready!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// In this context, `this` is the player that was created by Video.js.</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">play</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

  <span class="pl-c">// How about an event listener?</span>
  <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">on</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'ended'</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-k">function</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">videojs</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">log</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s">'Awww...over so soon?!'</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
  <span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
<span class="pl-kos">}</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span></pre></div>
<p dir="auto">If you're ready to dive in, the <a href="https://videojs.com/getting-started/" rel="nofollow">Getting Started</a> page and <a href="https://docs.videojs.com" rel="nofollow">documentation</a> are the best places to go for more information. If you get stuck, head over to our <a href="http://slack.videojs.com" rel="nofollow">Slack channel</a>!</p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-contributing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Contributing</h2>
<p dir="auto">Video.js is a free and open source library, and we appreciate any help you're willing to give - whether it's fixing bugs, improving documentation, or suggesting new features. Check out the <a href="/videojs/video.js/blob/main/CONTRIBUTING.md">contributing guide</a> for more!</p>
<p dir="auto"><em>Video.js uses <a href="https://browserstack.com" rel="nofollow">BrowserStack</a> for compatibility testing.</em></p>
<h2 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-code-of-conduct" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#code-of-conduct"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a><a href="/videojs/video.js/blob/main/CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md">Code of Conduct</a></h2>
<p dir="auto">Please note that this project is released with a <a href="/videojs/video.js/blob/main/CODE_OF_CONDUCT.md">Contributor Code of Conduct</a>. By participating in this project you agree to abide by its terms.</p>
